    display: inline;

        }

          --mr-toggled-font-family: Monospace;
        }
        .container-issue {
          width: 100%;
          flex-direction: column;
          align-items: stretch;

          z-index: 200;

        }

          height: calc(100vh - var(--monorail-header-height));
        }

            width: 100%;

Email display settings

<h2>Email display settings</h2>



        

There is a 

setting

<a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a>

 to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.

<p>There is a <a href="/hosting/settings">setting</a> to control how
        your email address appears on comments and issues that you post.</p>



        

Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.

<p>Project members will always see your full email address.  By
        default, other users who visit the site will see an
        abbreviated version of your email address.</p>



        

If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to 

get
        involved

<a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a>

 in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.

<p>If you do not wish your email address to be shared, there
        are other ways to <a href="http://www.chromium.org/getting-involved">get
        involved</a> in the community.  To report a problem when using
        the Chrome browser, you may use the "Report an issue..."  item
        on the "Help" menu.</p>

This site hosts public issues in public projects

<h2>This site hosts public issues in public projects</h2>



        

Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.

<p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>



        

Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.

<p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

        <p>Unlike our internal issue tracker, this site makes most
        issues public, unless the issue is labeled with a Restrict-View-*
        label, such as Restrict-View-Google.</p>

        <p>Components are not used for permissions.  And, regardless of
        restriction labels, the issue reporter, owner,
        and Cc'd users may always view the issue.</p>

<span class="line"><!---->2. Click on the calendar view in the bottom right corner of chromeOS<!----></span>

It seems like the scoped observer may be causing uaf errors during close calendar window, as the underlying source may be being deleted beforehand.



<span class="line"><!---->It seems like the scoped observer may be causing uaf errors during close calendar window, as the underlying source may be being deleted beforehand.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] CalendarEventListView observes CalendarViewController through |scoped_calendar_view_controller_observer_|



<span class="line"><!---->[1] CalendarEventListView observes CalendarViewController through |scoped_calendar_view_controller_observer_|<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[2] During calendar window close, |calendar_view_controller_| will be destroyed, but |scoped_calendar_view_controller_observer_| will nerver be reset.



<span class="line"><!---->[2] During calendar window close, |calendar_view_controller_| will be destroyed, but |scoped_calendar_view_controller_observer_| will nerver be reset.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[3] Then, when the |scoped_calendar_view_controller_observer_| is being destroyed, calling |calendar_view_controller_->RemoveObserver| will trigger the UAF.



<span class="line"><!---->[3] Then, when the |scoped_calendar_view_controller_observer_| is being destroyed, calling |calendar_view_controller_-&gt;RemoveObserver| will trigger the UAF.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





[1] 



<span class="line"><!---->[1] <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/system/time/calendar_event_list_view.cc;l=157;drc=169c6cc102b39295a5bfe2f2a176b42b1c2fe2c4



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/system/time/calendar_event_list_view.cc;l=157;drc=169c6cc102b39295a5bfe2f2a176b42b1c2fe2c4"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/system/time/calendar_event_list_view.cc;l=157;drc=169c6cc102b39295a5bfe2f2a176b42b1c2fe2c4<!----></a>



<br>





[2] 



<span class="line"><!---->[2] <!----></span>





https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/system/time/calendar_event_list_view.h;drc=169c6cc102b39295a5bfe2f2a176b42b1c2fe2c4;l=46



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/system/time/calendar_event_list_view.h;drc=169c6cc102b39295a5bfe2f2a176b42b1c2fe2c4;l=46"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:ash/system/time/calendar_event_list_view.h;drc=169c6cc102b39295a5bfe2f2a176b42b1c2fe2c4;l=46<!----></a>

<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:base/scoped_observation.h;l=70;drc=169c6cc102b39295a5bfe2f2a176b42b1c2fe2c4;bpv=1;bpt=1"><!---->https://source.chromium.org/chromium/chromium/src/+/main:base/scoped_observation.h;l=70;drc=169c6cc102b39295a5bfe2f2a176b42b1c2fe2c4;bpv=1;bpt=1<!----></a>

Let's consider CalendarView's destructor, if event_list_view_ is not empty and event_list_view_animator is not in is_animating state, then our calling sequence is:

At this point we can find that CalendarViewController destructs before CalendarEventListView, resulting in the UAF vulnerability described in 



<span class="line"><!---->At this point we can find that CalendarViewController destructs before CalendarEventListView, resulting in the UAF vulnerability described in <!----></span>





#c2



<a class="undefined" target="_blank" href="#c2"><!---->#c2<!----></a>





.



<span class="line"><!---->.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>





So here we can fix this vulnerability: just make sure that CalendarEventListView always destructs before CalendarViewController.



<span class="line"><!---->So here we can fix this vulnerability: just make sure that CalendarEventListView always destructs before CalendarViewController.<!----></span>



<br>



<br>
